42597332|Agave jarucoensis es descrita como una nueva especie endmica de Cuba Occidental, que crece sobre rocas y farallones calizos de la zona de Escaleras de Jaruco. Esta especie muestra su relacin ms estrecha con A. papyriocarpa Trel., de la que difiere por su mayor vigor, sus flores ms largas y sus cpsulas de paredes ms fuertes. A. jarucoensis A. Alvarez is described as a new endemic species from the occidental part of Cuba, growing upon limestone rocks and cliffs of Escaleras de Jaruco zone. Its closest relationship appears to be with A. papyriocarpa Trel. from which it mainly differs in its greater stout; its longer flowers and its stronger capsule wall.
42597333|Harrisia taetra es descrita como especie nueva de los acantilados costeros de caliza coralina, altamente carsificada, de la pennsula de Guanahacabibes, en el extremo occidental de Cuba. Sus relaciones ms cercanas las muestra con H. eriophora, de la que difiere sustancialmente en el mayor grosor de sus artculos; sus areolas mas prximas y ms espinosas; las espinas ms fuertes y largas, casi completamente negras cuando jvenes; sus tubos florales de color vinceo a verderrojo o rosado, de tpalos triangular-subulados, reducidos. Se ofrece una clave para las especies cubanas de Harrisia, hasta el presente conocidas. Harrisia taetra is newly described from the coastal steep cliffs of highly carsified quaternary coral-limestone of the Guanahacabibes peninsula, extreme western part of Cuba. Its closest relationship appears to be with H. eriophora from which it mainly differs in its thicker joints; its closer and more spiny areoles; its stouter and longer spines which are almost black when young; its vinaceous' to githaginaceous orpink flower tubes with reduced triangular-subulate tepals. A key to the Cuban known species of Harrisia is provided.

42596602|Sierra del Turquino is the highest group of mountains of the country. It goes all along the southern coast of Granma and Santiago de Cuba provinces. This region stands in a very peculiar position in the cuban flora because of the presence of strict endemicals and the andean elements which are part-of macrodisjunction. The floristic associations in this region go from "mountain rain forest" to "subalpine fresh thicket forest" according to the altitude. Something very interesting is the relocalization of Miconiapteroclada Urb. La Sierra del Turquino presenta las mayores elevaciones delpas extendindose paralelamente a la costa sur de las provincias Granma y Santiago de Cuba. Esta regin ocupa una posicin importante en la flora cubana por la presencia de endmicos estrictos y elementos andinos que forman parte demacrodis junciones. Las asociaciones florsticas que se presentan van desde pluviosilvas de montaa hasta monte fresco en dependencia de la altura en que se localizan.

42596692|Die Gattung Coccoloba L. ist mit rund 150 Arten in der Neotropis verbreitet. Die meisten Arten besiedeln nur ein kleines Teilgebiet des Gattungsareals. Nach der Artenzahl in verschiedenen Teilgebieten des Gattungsareals heben sich Hufungszentren heraus, die einen hohen Anteil an endemischen Arten besitzen. Mit anderen Zentren haben sie oft nur wenige Arten gemeinsam. Deshalb werden die Hufungszentren als Entfaltungszentren der Gattung gedeutet. The genus Coccoloba L. occurs with about 150 species in the Neotropics. The majority of the species is found only in a small part of the generic area. In several parts of the generic area the number of species indicates centres of accumulation, which are characterized by a high percentage of endemic species. In general they have in common with other centres a few species only. Therefore the centres of accumulation are interpreted as centres of evolution of the genus. El gnero Coccoloba L. posee alrededor de 150 especies en los neotrpicos. La mayora de las especies se encuentran solamente en una pequea parte del areal del gnero. En algunas partes de este areal, el nmero de especies indica centros de acumulacin, los cuales estn caracterizados por un alto porciento de especies endmicas; y en general, ellos tienen en comn con otros centros unas pocas especies solamente. Por esta razn los centros de acumulacin son interpretados como centros de evolucin del gnero.

42596739|En el presente trabajo se describen los caracteres anatmicos de la madera de Brunellia comocladifolia H. & B. (nico representante de Brunelliaceae. en Cuba). 42596761|Se evaluaron los contenidos de N, P, K, Ca y Mg en las races y el follaje de plntulas de Hibiscus elatus Sw. cultivados durante 112 das en suelo rojo ferraltico al que se aplicaron tres niveles; de N (0, 100 y 200 mg) 2 de P (0 y 100 mg) y 2 de K (0 y, 100 mg). La adicin de N increment en general los contenidos de nitrgeno, fsforo, potasio, calcio y magnesio, mientras que el suministro de P no produjo variaciones apreciables en estos nutrientes con excepcin del magnesio que aument su contenido. El K anadido no produjo cambios sustanciales en los valores de nitrgeno, fsforo y potasio y provoc una ligera disminucin de los tenores de calcio y magnesio. El N, K y Ca, al parecer se absorben y trasladan de forma rpida hacia las partes areas de la planta. Con excepcin del magnesio el mayor tenor mineral se registr en el follaje. The added K did not sustantially changed the contents of nitrogen, phosphorus or potassium but slightly decreased the contents of calcium and magnesium. N, K and Ca seems to be uptaken and translated in a repid way to the upper parts of the plants. Except for magnesium, the greater content of minerals was found for the shoots. A good answers to the addition of 100 mg of N and of K were found, in terms of the nutrients analyzed and no answer to phosphoric fertilization could be established. The addition of 100 mg of N and of K is recommended for the conditions in which the experiment was carried out and the necessary profundization into the nutritional requirements of this species is pointed out.

42596622|Se evaluaron los contenidos de N, P, K, Ca y Mg en las races y el follaje de plntulas de Hibiscus elatus Sw. cultivadas durante 112 das en suelo Amarillo Tropical Tipico al que se aplicaron tres nive les de N(0, 100 y 200 mg/kg de suelo) 2 de P(O y 100 mg) y 2 de K(O y 100 mg). En general la adicin de nitrgeno favoreci la absorcin de nutrientes con excepcin del potasio que result disminuido. El fsforo aunque no produjo cambios sustanciales en su contenido, al parecer mejor la disponibilidad y absorcin del nitrgeno y favoreci la absorcin del magnesio; mentras que el potasio disminuy ligeramente la absorcin del nitrgeno y present la mayor respuesta en trminos de su contenido. Though its plant contents did not significantly change when added to the soil, phosphorus apparently improved the nitrogen availability and uptake and favoured the uptake of magnesium; besides the addicion of potassium lightly diminished the nitrogen uptake and, in terms of its own plant content showed the highest response. Nitrogen, potassium, calcium and magnesium uptakes and translocations likely occurred rapidly upward to the shoot; phosphorus, however, irregularly distibuted in the plant. Results are descussed in light of the plant development. That nutrient added proportions were not apropiated for establishing an adequate balance between them is concluded.

42597475|En 1866, A. Grisebach estableci un nuevo gnero al describir Henoonia myrtifolia, que incluy en Sapotaceae, a pesar de encontrarlo afn con Myroinaceae. Numerosos autores han dado diversas interpretaciones filogenticas a este gnero, que adems ha transitado por las familias Solanaceae y Goetzeaceae. La revisin de esta ltima familia que se realiza para la redaccin de la Flora de la Repblica de Cuba, ha mostrado la invalidez del nombre genrico Henoonia, al existir dos gneros homnimos ms antiguos, por lo que se propone el nombre de Bissea, en honor al Dr. Johannes Bisse, eminente conocedor de la flora cubana. In 1866, A. Grisebach established a new genus describing Henoonia myrtifolia, which he included among Sapotaceae, in spite of the affinities to Myruinaceae which he also found. Many authors have given to this genus different filogenetical interpretations, considering it as if it were indistinctly a species of the family Colanaccae or Goetzeaceae. Wile reviewing the family Goetzeaceae for the Flora of the Republic of Cuba, we realized the invalidity of the generic name Henoonia because of the existence of two eldest homonymus genus, proposing a new name, Bissea, to honor Dr. Johannes Bisse, a brillant knower of the Cuban flora.

42597485|Se evaluaron los contenidos de N,P,K, Ca y Mg en las races y el follaje de plntulas de Hibiscus clatus Sw. cultivadas durante 112 das en suelo Ferraltico Rojo lixiviado al que se aplicaron tres niveles de N(0, 100 y 200 mg) 2 de K(0 y 100 mg). La adicin de 100 mg de N favoreci la absorcin del nitrgeno en todas las combinaciones empleadas. La fertilizacin fosfrica mejor la absorcin del calcio, el magnesio y el fsforo. Por otra parte la aplicacin de NP (100 mg de cada elemento) parece aconsejable debido al incremento obtenido en la productividad de la planta. El potasio present la mayor respuesta en trminos de su contenido y en general no favoreci la absor cin de los elementos estudiados. El nitrgeno, el potasio y el calcio, al parecer, se absorben y trasladan de forma rpida hacia las partes areas de las plantas mientras que el fsforo y el magnesio no presentaron comportamientos que puedan ser generalizados. Root and shoot contents of N,P,K, Ca and Mg were estimated in Ilibiscus elatus Sw. plants grown during 112 days on an Ferralitico Rojo Lixiviado soil ammended with three levels of N(0, 100 and 200 mg/kg of soil), 2 of P (0 and 100 mg/kg of soil), and 2 of k (0. and 100mg/kg of soil) which were previously added. The addition of 100 mg N favoured the N uptake at all the added proportions, the phosphate fertilization improved the calcium, magnesium and phosphorus uptakes. Besides the addition of combines N and P (100 mg of each element) seemed to be advisable due to the resulting plant productivity improvement. Potassium when added showed the highest response in terms of its own plant content and generally did not improve the uptake of other elements. Nitrogen, potassium and calcium uptakes and translocations likely occurred rapidly upward to the shoots while phosphorus and magnesium did not show tipical behaviours to realize generalizations.

42597553|Se calcularon los ciclos de nutrientes en el sistema detritus-suelo sobre la base de los datos previamente obtenidos de tasa de descomposicin de la hojarasca, contenido de nutrientes de la hojarasca y el suelo, y respiracin del suelo. Los ciclos del C, N, P y K calculados mostraron dos estrategias diferentes en los ecosistemas estudiados. En la plantacin de Hibiecue elatus, la produccin es ms dependiente de los nutrientes rpidamente liberados en la descomposicin de la hojarasca. En el bosque natural, existe una reserva de nutrientes en la hojarasca acumulada en el horizonte Ao, la hojarasca se descompone ms lentamente y la existencia de una estera radical asegura la retencin de los nutrientes liberados de la hojarasca en descomposicin. Based on the previously obtained data concerning litter descomposition rate, litter and soil nutrient content and soil respiration, C, N, P and K ciclings were calculated in the soil-detritus system in two forests: a natural one, corresponding to a tropical evergreen submontane forest and a Hibiscus elatus plantation of 10 years. Two different cicling strategies were found. That of the plantation based in a rapid turnover, in which production is more dependent on the nutrients released in litter decomposition, and that of the natural forest, in which there is a nutrient pool in the litter accumulated in A horizon, litter decomposition is slower and a root mat plays an important role in conserving nutrients released from decomposing litter.

42596812|Se determinaron las caractersticas de crecimiento de cinco mutantes de diferenciacin de Aspergillus nidulans a cuatro temperaturas diferentes. S estableci que las mutaciones que definen el fallo en la diferenciacin muestran un efecto pleiotrpico sobre el crecimiento. Mutantes con este tipo de efecto no han sido antes descritos. Se identific para cada mutante un patrn de comportamiento temperatura especfico, aungue en general a temperatura superior a la ptima de crecimiento, no se observ tal efecto. The growth characteristics of five differentiation mutants of Aspergillus nidulans at four different temperatures were determined. It was established that the mutations determining differentiation failure had a pleiotropic effect over growth. Mutants with such type of pleiotropic effect have not been described before. For each mutant a specific pattern of temperature dependent behavior was identified, although in general supraoptimum growth temperature failed to elicit a pleiotropic effect.

42596840|El ms reciente estudio monogrfico de las especies cubanas de Solanceas es el publicado por Jane Amshoff en 1957 para la "Flora de Cuba" de Len y Alain (1946-1964). Desde entonces hasta la fecha, se han descrito nuevas especies, y ha sido necesario realizar algunos cambios de nomenclatura, e inclusive, de familia. La preparacin de la "Flora de la Repblica de Cuba" ha permitido la revisin de esta familia de amplia representacin en nuestro pas. A pesar de que los estudios realizados no han sido concluidos contamos hasta el presente con 100 especies nativas o naturalizadas, 33 de las cuales son endmicas, agrupadas en 18 gneros; sin incluir unas 10 especies cultivadas con fines econmicos u ornamentales. Estas especies se agrupan en dos subfamilias: Solanoideae, con 4 tribus que comprenden 65 especies, de las cuales 14 son endmicas; y Cestroideae, con 35 especies que incluyen 19 endmicas. The most recent monographic study about the Cuban species of Solanaceae is the one published by Jane Amshoff in "Flora of Cuba" by Len and Alain (1946-1964). Up to date, new species have been described, and some changes of nomenclature have been found necessary, and even, family changes. The preparation of "Flora of the Republic of Cuba" has made possible a review of this family, widely represented in our Country. Although the studied have not been concluded, we have actually 100 species, grouped in 18 genus, native or naturalized; 33 of these species are endemical. There exist about 10 species, cultivated for economical and ornamental purposes wich were not considered in our study. The species are grouped in two sub-families: Solanoideae, having 4 tribes with 65 species, (14 of them endemical) and Cestroideae, having 35 species (19 of them endemical). The future studied on this family, undoubtedly will determine changes of great significance in its actual status.

42596851|En este trabajo se proponen nuevos limites para la regin del Caribe, la que se divide en tres subregiones: Amrica Central, Antillas y Colombia-Venezuela septentrional, debido a la soberana de sus floras. La subregin de Amrica Central se divide en cuatro provincias: Islas Revillagigedo, Costa Pacfica de Amrica Central, Golfo de Mxico y Guatemala-Panam. La subregin de las Antillas se divide en seis provincias: Bermudas-Bahamas y Florida Meridional, Cuba, Espaola, Puerto Rico, Jamaica y Antillas Menores. Por ltimo la subregin de Colombia-Venezuela septentrional se propone como una sola provincia, aunque tal vez se podran considerar dos provincias: Colombia-Venezuela septentrional y Trinidad-Tobago, pero an no se tienen todos los elementos para justificar esa divisin por falta de conocimientos de la flora de esta zona. Se hacen descripciones de las subregiones y las priovincias y se ponen ejemplos de gneros y especies propias de cada una de ellas. New limits are proposed for the Caribbean region, divided into three subregin: Central America, Antillas and Northern Colombia-Venezuela, due to sovereighty of their florae. The Subreqian of Central America is divided into four provincesl Revilla gigedo isles, Pacific Coast of Central America, Gulf of Mxico and Guatemala-Panam. The Antilles subregion is divided into six provinces: Bermudas-Bahamas and Southern Florida, Cuba, Espaola, Puerto Rico, Jamaica and Lesser Antilles. Finally, the subregion of Northern Colombia-Venezuela is proposed as a sole province, even though two could be considered: Northern Colombia-Venezuela and Trinidad-Tobago, but at present there is not enough criterion to justify this division on behalf of a lack knowledge on the flora of this region. Descriptions of subregion and provinces with examples of distinctive genera and species of each one, are given.

42596858|Se estudia la ecologa reproductiva del Sinsonte (Mimus poliglottos orpheus) en la zona de Manigua Costera del Jardin Botnico Nacional entre los meses de febrero y agosto de 1987. A mediados de -febrero comienza la delimitacin de los territorios y la formacin de las parejas, mientras que la elaboracin de los primeros nidos ocurre en el mes de marzo y la puesta a principios de abril. La incubacin dura entre 13 y 14 dias. La altura promedio de los nidos fue de 2,09 m y en todos los casos utilizaron arbustos espinosos y muy ramificados como sustrato. Generalmente efectan una segunda nidada a partir del mes de mayo. The reproductive ecology o-F Northern Mockingbird (Mimus poliglottos orpheus) in the Coastal Thorny Thicket of the National Botanic Garden was studied between february and august 1987. About the middle of february began the pairs formation and the territorial delimitation, while the first nests appeared in march and the first laying in early april. The incubation period lasted between 13 and 14 days. The average height of the nests was 2,09 m and all of them were constructed in thorny branched shrubs. A second laying began in may.

Cuba is considered one of the richest in palm species in the world, and in Central Cuba, the main distribution area of palms in the country is found. Of the 28 known species of Copernicia in the world, 23 belong to Cuba and 10 of them have been reported from Sancti Spiritus province. The Copernicia especies have economical significance since a great variety of palm leaves are obtained for craftmanship and rural constructions. Information concerning morphology, phenology and geographical localization of the species within the province are given, and some actions that should be taken for conservation are proposed. A key for identification of Copernicia species within the province is also given.

Se analizan adems las fluctuaciones en la biomasa de cada uno de los gremios presentes. Para todos los parmetros se present la misma tendencia con dos picos a lo largo del ao, aunque existen alqunas diferencias en cuanto a la posicin de los mismos. Asi puede apreciarse que para la riqueza especfica y la diversidad los puntos culminantes son enero y octubre, mientras que para la densidad y biomasa fueron en febrero o marzo respectivamente y agosto. Variations in the annual cycle of the species richness, density, diversity, equitativity and biomass were studied in the 3 groups of birds in the community: permanent residents, winter residents and summer residents. Fluctuations in biomass were analized in the different guilds. All parameters showed the same tendency throughout the year with two maximun values that were found in january and october for the species richness and diversity, while in density and biomass the higher values were observed in february or march, and august.

42596886|Variaciones de algunos caracteres florales encontradas en el estudio de materiales de herbario de poblaciones de Vaccinium cubense Griseb. de Cuba y La Espaola, junto a la distribucin geogrfica relativamente aislada de las mismas, indican la existencia de diferentes taxa dentro de este grupo. The author proposes the following treatment: for western Cuba the name Vaccinium ramonii Griseb. was revalidated and Lectotipified the species; for central Cuba a new species is described: Vaccinium bissei Berazan; for eastern Cuba two varieties of Vaccinium cubense Griseb. are recognized: Vaccinium cubense Griseb. var cubense and Vaccinium cubense Griseb. var giganteum (Bisse) Berazan. Actually, 873 taxa in extinction are reported (the 14,2 % and 27,7 %. of the total of species and endemics, respectively). Definitions of the categories of threat and the quantities of plants in extinction by provinces are offered.

42596914|A pesar de que se conoce la diversidad y composicin de la flora de nuestro pas, no se ha diferenciado de entre las especies indgenas (endmicas y nativas) que no resisten el impacto antrpico, las que s lo resisten, y las introducidas que se encuentran estrechamente vinculadas a las actividades del hombre, y que revisten gran importancia dado el alto porcentaje de deforestacin de nuestro pas. Con el fin de conocer las especies sinantrpicas se adapt la clasificacin de Kornas modificada por Rousseau para las condiciones insulares tropicales de Cuba, realizndose los aportes siguientes: (1) la divisin de la categora intrapfitos en Intrapfitos ploneros, para las especies que intervienen en el proceso sucesional, e intrapfitos recuperadores para las que recuperan el habitat original despus de su destruccin; (2) creacin del trmino parapfitos para aquellas de origen desconocido, y (3) se propone una nueva definicin del trmino especie sinantrpica. Although the composition and diversity of the Cuban flora are well known, no attempt has been made to separate native (including endemics) species which are intolerant of man activities from those that can overcome such handicap whether native or introduced, that have become troublesome weeds depending on the high Cuban rates of deforestation. In order to accomplish this and also in order to list the synanthropics species of Cuba, the classification system of Korna (emendavit Rousseau) was adopted and applied under Cuban insularity and tropical conditions. As a consequence, the following results were obtained: (1) Intrapophytes were divided in pioneer intrapophytes (those species which play a major role in sucesional processes), recuperationist intrapophytes (species which are able to adapt themselves to man impact without any need of sucesional stages), and intrapophytes (sensu stricto) which can hardly tolerate deforestation; (2) a new term, parapophytes: synanthropics species of unknown origin, is proposed; (3) a new definition of synanthropic species is given.

42596929|Cissampelos L. (Menispermaceae, Cocculeae) agrupa unas 20 especies tropicales y subtropicales, en su casi totalidad lianas subherbceas o subfrutescentes, marcadamente heteromorfas en cuanto a arquitectura foliar y tipos de inflorescencias. (Menispermaceae, Cocculeae) about 20 tropical and subtropical species are grouped, mainly subherbaceus or subfrutescent liana, greatly heteromorphic in reference to their foliar architecture and inflorescence types. 42597000|A partir del estudio morfoanatmico de las especies cubanas de Begonia se detecta una estrecha relacin entre la organizacin de los estomas y la arquitectura transversal de la lmina foliar. En las especies que poseen los estomas agrupados, se pierde la individualidad de la cmara subestomtica formndose una estructura nica de dimetro equivalente al ancho del grupo de estomas la cual fue observada por Boghdan y Barkley en 1972 sin otorgrsele nombre. En el presente trabajo, la nueva estructura es nombrada Cmara Subestomtica Mltiple (CSM). La CSM responde a una adaptacin fisiolgica y ecomorfolgica para la regulacin de la transpiracin cuya estrategia es analizada por vez primera. Morphoanatomical studies of cuban species of Begonia show a close relation between stomatal patterns and leaf transversal architecture. A ship common one chamber is found for grouped stomata when they occur in cluster. This chamber was observed by Boghdan and Barkley in 1972 but it was not named. In this paper the structure is named as Multiple Stomatal Chamber (MSC). The diameter of MSC is similar in size to the stomatal cluster and it is a physiological and ecomorphological adaptation in controlling transpiration, a strategy analized for the first time.

42597003|Una postura joven (alrededor de 20 mm de altura) de Ficus hemsleyana Standley fue colectada en el Campus de la Universidad de Sao Paulo (Riberao Preto, Brasil) en 1984 y plantada en el Campus de la Universidad de Costa Rica. La postura creci normalmente hasta ser un rbol, el cual floreci por primera vez en 1994. Sus sconos fueron polinizados por avispas : Pegoscapus tonduzi (Grandi) (Agaonidae), el polinizador de F. hemsleyana Standley en Amrica Central. Tambin se desarrollan normalmente en las flores del rbol las avispas inquilinas Idarnes barbigera Gordh y Anidarmes sp., los parsitos Heterandrium sp. (Otitesellinae) y un Pteromalidae sp. Esto marca la especificidad de las avispas polinizadoras y otras sicofilas y la probable ausencia de ecotipos para las avispas y su ficus hospedero ; cada siconio produce un promedio de 150 avispas polinizadoras y 85 semillas. Las semillas se desarrollan y crecen normalmente. Aparentemente no hay mecanismos de aislamiento gentico entre el rbol brasileo introducido y la poblacin natural de Costa Rica de F. hemsleyana. Las poblaciones mesoamericanas y de Sur Amrica de F. hemsleyana no corresponden con F. laevigata Vohl, el cual es una especie indgena de la Florida. El rbol brasileo y la poblacin mesoamericana de F. hemsleyana se incluyen en la descripcin de F. citrifolia P. Mill, (sinnimo de F. hemsleyana) para los especmenes de Costa Rica. A young seedling (about 20 mm high) of Ficus hemsleyana Standley was collected at the Campus of the University of Sao Paulo (Riberao Preto, Brazil) in 1984 and planted at the Campus of the University of Costa Rica. The seedling grew normally into a tree that first bloomed in 1994. Its syconia were pollinated by Pegoscapus tonduzi (Grandi) wasps (Agaonidae), the pollinator of F. hemsleyana Stand, in Central America. The inquiline wasps Idarnes barbigera Gordh and Anidarnes sp. (Sycophaginae), the parasitic Heterandrium sp. (Otitesellinae) and a Pteromalidae sp. also developed normally in the flowers of the tree. This points to the specificity of the pollinating and other sycophilous wasps and the probable absence of ecotypes for the wasps and their fig host. Each syconia produced an average of 150 pollinating wasps and 85 seeds. The seeds developed and germinated normally. Apparently there was no genetic isolating mechanisms between the introduced Brazilian tree and the Costa Rican natural population of F. hemsleyana. The Mesoamerican and South American populations of F. hemsleyana do not correspond to F. laevigata Vahl, which is an indigenous species of Florida. The Brazilian tree and the Mesoamerican population of F. hemsleyana fit the description of F. citrifolia P. Mill, (synonym of F. hemsleyana) for Costa Rican specimens.

Urb. regenerated in a natural way departing from seeds produced by trees beloging to these species, which were located in the farthest borders of this Center. About 30 years after the area was left resting so that the forest could arise from natural succession, an inventory was made in order to know the frequency and the spatial distribution of these plant offspring. The information was obtained from 36 m lots systematically allocated in the areas and a general botanical collection which also allowed to know the flora composition and the natural regeneration of other important species. Brosimum alicastrum could uniformly cover 87,5% of the area with about 47 770 plants standing for approximately 1,4 plant per m, while Trophis racemosa settled in 37,5% of the area with about 15 690 plants, with 1,04 individuals per m, these results being very interesting for its use in forestenrichment works using natural regeneration.

Disinfection scheme combining the Cuban product BENZALCONIO with alcohol and commercial sodium hypochloride for obtention of highly satisfactory results (>98%) was established; the effect of nutritive medium and culture conditions previously applied to Fragaria  ananasa (Martnez et al., 1985) for initiating shoot formation in four weeks was proved; the possibility of three subcultures of initiated material without vitrification in more than 95% of the resulting vitroplants was obtained; and that the tested substrate (humus: silica sand in proportion 2:1) and conditions applied for acclimatization and initial growth in tunnel conditions are effective in 100%. Results are discussed.

Lam., Jatropha curcas L, Ocimum basilicum L., Ocimum tenuiflorum L., Ricinus communis L., Sesamum orientale L. The general technique of phytochemical screening described by Rondina and Coussio was used. Triterpens and steroids were present in 100 %; reducing sugars, in 93,75 %; flavonoids, in 68,7 %; and phenols, in 62,5 % of the evaluated species. Tannins, quiones, cardenolids and cianogenic glycosides were not detected in the samples.
42597055|Sobre la base de la revisin bibliogrfica y de los datos tomados de las etiquetas de herbario, se distinguen dos perodos en la historia de la Botnica en la provincia de Camagey, Cuba: el primero, entre 1797 y 1979, denominado "florstico", porque prevaleci el inters por el estudio de la flora, con una escasa participacin de instituciones e investigadores locales, por lo que las principales contribuciones fueron resultado de expediciones ocasionales organizadas desde la capital del pas o desde el extranjero, para colectar material vegetal en un limitado nmero de localidades en que mejor conservada se encontraba la flora y vegetacin original. El segundo, denominado "perodo integral", desde 1980 hasta el presente, en que se ha logrado el desarrollo de mltiples ramas de esta ciencia, los principales aportes los han realizado instituciones e investigadores locales dedicados permanentemente a la investigacin, al custodio de colecciones y a la divulgacin de conocimientos. Se anexa una cronologa de los principales sucesos, as como tablas con datos de los colectores y de las localidades estudiadas durante la primera etapa. In the history of Botany in the province of Camagey, it is possible to distinguish two periods: The first, between 1797 and 1979, may be named "floristic period", because its the most important objective was the study of the flora. The second, from 1980 to the present day, may be named "integral period", because many branches of this science have undergone an important development. In the first period, the native institutions and botanists had very little participation in the researches, and the main contribution were made by expeditions organized from Havana or from abroad. For this reason, very few localities were studied and the specimens were not conserved in the provincial herbaria. In the second period, the main contributions have been realized by regional institutions, the collection and conservation of specimens as well as the spread of knowledge was increased. In this article, a great deal of data of the main researches, botanists, and localities studied, are anexed in chronological order.

42597095|En Cuba los campesinos tradicionalmente han mantenido sus variedades, pero no de una manera esttica, sino incluyendo en ese mantenimiento una seleccin consciente o inconsciente orientada en dos direcciones: la primera hacia el mantenimiento del tipo de planta deseado (reproduccin de la variedad ancestral) y la segunda hacia el cambio de la misma mediante la seleccin de determinados atributos que llenen los requerimientos que les van imponiendo las condiciones cambiantes del medio donde se desarrolla la planta. De esta manera, la conservacin de este patrimonio gentico, rico en atributos de adaptacin, supervivencia y rusticidad, requiere de un sistema informal, que no implique un conjunto de pasos pre-determinados hasta llegar a la semilla comercial. Se describen en el trabajo las diferentes variantes en la produccin de semilla en huertos caseros de las zonas occidental y central de Cuba, as como se particulariza en algunos de los procedimientos tradicionales empleados por los campesinos. Farmers in Cuba have traditionally maintained their varieties, not in a static way, but including in their maintenance conscious and unconscious selection, addressed in two directions: the first, towards the maintenance of the desired plant type (reproduction of the ancestral variety), and the second towards their change by means of selection on specific attributes that fullfil new requirements imposed by changes of the environment where the plant develops. So, the conservation of this genetic patrimony, rich in adaptation, survival and rusticity attributes, requires an informal seed production system that doesn't imply a set of pre-determined steps in order to produce the commercial seeds. In the present article, the different variants for seed production in home gardens from Western and Central part of Cuba are described, as well as, some traditional procedures used by farmers are emphasized.

The litter was sorted in leaves, fruits, bark and climber fragments, the biological type were determinated wherever possible. The microarthopods were extracted by means of Berlese-Tullgren funnels. A total of 37 plant species was identified, and it was found some structural and floristic differences between subplots, due to the complexity of vegetation and flora of subplot B. In the litter were collected 27 species and the proportion of biological types corresponds to the composition of the forest. Microarthopods densities were significantly lower in subplot A than in subplot B, this result may reflects the differences in the vegetation structure and flora in both subplots. Existe poca informacin sobre la abundancia de mircoartrpodos edficos en relacin con la composicin y estrucura de la hojarasca. Se llevaron a cabo 7 mustreos con periodicidad quincenal desde enero a abril de 1999 en dos subparcelas (A y B) de un bosque semideciduo estacional localizado en el Bosque Municipl de So Jos de Rio Preto, Estado de Sao Paulo, Brasil, La hojarasca se clasific en hojas, frutos, fragmentos de corteza y lianas. Los microartrpodos se extrajeron mediante embudos Berlese-Tullgen. Se identificaron 37 especies de plantas asi como sus tipos biolgicos. Las diferencias entre las dos subaparcelas se deben a la complejidad estructural y a la flora presente en la subparcela B. En la hojarasca se colectaron e identificaron 27 especies, la proporcin de sus tipos biolgicos se corresponde con la composicin estrucutral del bosque. Las densidades de microartrpodos fueron significativamente mas bajas en la subparcela A, lo que refleja las diferencias en la estructura de la vegetacin y la flora entre las dos subaprcelas.
42597118|Se analiza la posible relacin entre la especificidad por la planta hospedante y la taxonoma en Meliolales, a partir de colectas peridicas en un rea seleccionada del Jardn Botnico Nacional. Los resultados obtenidos apuntan a que existe una real especificidad por el hospedante (al menos a nivel de familia), como se ha tratado tradicionalmente, ya que se evidencia una clara diferenciacin morfolgica entre los 11 taxa encontrados sobre 10 familias hospedantes. En consecuencia, se mantiene el criterio de que este es un elemento fundamental en la sistemtica del grupo. The supposed relationship between host specificity and taxonomy in Meliolales is analysed through periodic collections in a particular area of the National Botanical Garden. The results point out that exist a real host specificity (at least at family level), as traditional used, because a clear morphologic differentiation in 11 taxa on 10 host families is evidenced. Therefore, the criterion that it is an essential element in the systematic of the group should be maintained.

This paper is a comparative study among eight conucos of Pinar del Ro and Cienfuegos provinces (four in each one). 42597128|La flora de la Sierra del Infierno, Cordillera de Guaniguanico, se corresponde con el Complejo de vegetacin de mogote segn listas florsticas reportadas para esta formacin vegetal. Las comunidades vegetales de este complejo de vegetacin fueron muestreadas en junio del 2000. Los anlisis de las variables discretas correspondientes a las especies muestreadas: subtipo geogrfico, hbito, condicin de endemismo y nivel de distribucin fitogeogrfica, respecto a las formaciones vegetales con las que se comparten especies presentan diferencias significativas. El subtipo geogrfico hoyo es el ms representado en la generalidad de las formaciones vegetales con taxa de distribucin provincial, a diferencia de la distrital que caracteriza a los subtipos paredn y cima. Los hbitos rbol y trepador son los ms representados. La generalidad de los taxa no son endemismos y los que presentan la condicin, generalmente arbustos, poseen mayores por cientos en Complejo de vegetacin de mogote y formaciones vegetales afines. Las variables subtipo geogrfico, hbito, condicin de amenaza y nivel de distribucin fitogeogrfica presentan diferencias significativas respecto a las familias determinadas para los taxa muestreados. El hoyo es el subtipo ms representado con mayor contribucin de Orchidaceae, Bromeliaceae, Euphorbiaceae y Rubiaceae. En cima adems de stas, tambin contribuyen Asteraceae, Cactaceae, Boraginaceae y Erythroxylaceae. Erythroxylaceae y Araceae lo hacen en paredn. El hbito rbol es el ms representado en Moraceae, Boraginaceae, Euphorbiaceae y Rubiaceae. Estas dos ltimas, adems de Asteraceae y Flacourtiaceae tienen altas contribuciones de arbustos. La generalidad de las familias no tiene especies amenazadas, excepto en el 22.81%. La amenaza es frecuente en endemismos y por ende en especies arbustivas de cima y paredn. Los niveles provincia y distrito fitogeogrfico estn ms representados en las familias, lo cual permite reconocer una distribucin sectorial y polar de la flora cubana occidental. La generalidad de las especies distritales son endemismos. Dada la diferenciacin de los subtipos geogrficos respecto a las variables analizadas, pueden reconocerse como potenciales subformaciones vegetales del Complejo de vegetacin de mogote. Based on published floral descriptions for the Sierra del Infierno, Cordillera de Guaniguanico, this formation is characterized as a mogote vegetational complex. We sampled vegetative communities in the mogote complex in June 2000. Analyses of these data revealed significant differences among plant associations and their shared species for the discrete variables of geographical sub-type, form, level of endemism, and phytogeographic distribution. Among the geographic sub-types, sinks had the highest representation of taxa with provincial distribution, compared with wall and summit sub-types. Among forms, trees and vines were best represented in our samples. The majority of taxa are nonendemics and those that are endemic, mostly shrubs, compose the major percentage of the vegetative complex of the mogote and similar plant formations. Representation of families of taxa encountered was significantly different among the geographical sub-types, plant form, degree of threat, and phytogeographical distribution variables. The sink was the best-represented sub-type with greatest contribution of the families Orchidaceae, Bromeliaceae, Euphorbiaceae, and Rubiaceae. In addition to these, the families Asteraceae, Cactaceae, Boraginaceae, and Erythroxylaceae were found on the summits, and Erythroxylaceae and Araceae on the mogote walls. The tree form was best represented by the families Moraceae, Boraginaceae, Euphorbiaceae, and Rubiaceae. The last two families, as well as the Asteraceae and Flacourtiaceae, also contributed to the shrub form. Among the represented families in the study area, 22.8% had species considered threatened. Endangerment is most frequent among endemics, particularly in shrub species occurring in the summit and wall sub-types. Families were best represented at the province and district levels, which allows determination of sector and polar distribution of the flora in western Cuba. The majority of the districtrestricted species are endemic forms. Given the differentiation of the geographic sub-types with respect to the variables we analyzed, these sub-types should be recognized as potential distinct plant subformations of the mogote vegetational complex.

42597134|Los brasinoesteroides constituyen un nuevo grupo de reguladores del crecimiento vegetal que tienen un marcado efecto sobre la recuperacin de las plantas bajo diferentes tipos de estrs. Se emplearon callos de caa de azcar que fueron sometidos a estrs abitico con manitol 20%, PEG-1500 20% y CINa 50 m molar. Las soluciones se prepararon en medio MS de regeneracin y los callos se colocaron en placas, sobre papel de filtro embebido en las soluciones, durante 7 das, en condiciones estriles. Al cabo de este tiempo se pasaron al medio slido MS con 24-epibrasinlido y los anlogos de brasinoesteroides Biobras-6 y Biobras-16. Se detect una respuesta positiva sobre el crecimiento del callo y la regeneracin de brotes a partir de los callos estresados y cultivados posteriormente con los brasinoesteroides. Se obtiene una respuesta diferencial entre el producto utilizado para provocar el estrs y el brasinoesteroide utilizado en su recuperacin. Brassinosteroids are a new group of plant growth regulators which an special effect on plant recuperation after different stress conditions. Sugarcane callus were stressed with mannitol 20%, PEG-1500 20% and NaCl 50 m molar solutions prepared on MS liquid media for plantlet regeneration. Callus were treated in petri dishes on filter paper embebed in different solutions, during 7days,in sterile conditions. After that, callus were transfered to solid MS media supplemented with 24-epibrassinolide and the synthetic brassinosteroid analogues Biobras-6 and Biobras-16. A positive reponse on callus growth and plantlet regeneration was detected. A differential reponse between stress substance and the brassinosteroid used for recuperation is obtained.

42597136|Para la mayora de las gramneas, la induccin del callo resulta esencial en la iniciacin de los cultivos y en el desencadenamiento de los eventos morfogenticos en condiciones in vitro. Semillas maduras de las variedades Jucarito-104 (J-104), Pokkali (Pok) e IACUBA-23 (IAC-23), previamente descascaradas y desinfectadas, constituyeron el explante inicial. Se probaron 4 combinaciones de medios de cultivo a partir de las sales de Murashige y Skoog (1962) (MS) y Chu et al., 1975 (N), el cido 2,4 -diclorofenoxiactico (2,4-D) 2.0 mg/L y la Kinetina (KIN) 1.0 mg/L y se efectuaron cortes histolgicos a los callos R resultantes. Los medios I y II favorecieron la callognesis y ejercieron una accin diferencial sobre la formacin de centros meristemticos y la diferenciacin de elementos traqueales. In most Gramineae, callus induction is essential to culture initiation and unleashing of in vitro morphogenetic events. Mature seeds of Jucarito-104 (J-104), Pokkali (Pok) and IACUBA-23 (IAC-23) varieties, previously husking and disinfected, were the initial explant. 4 combinations of culture media were tested, using Murashige and Skoog (1962) (MS) and Chu et al., 1975 (N) salts, 2,4 -dichlorophenoxyacetic acid (2,4-D) 2.0 mg/L and Kinetin (KIN) 1.0 mg/L and histologic cuts were performed on the resulting R callus. Callogenesis was enhanced by media I and II which had a differential effect on the formation of meristem centres and differentiation of tracheal elements.

In this paper preliminary tests were made in the field ("Cerrado", "Campo Sujo", "Mata ciliar" and "Brejo" formations), in Niquelndia, Gois state, using a semi-quantitative test with indicator paper (impregnated in dimethilglioxine in 10% in ethanol solution). In this work the existent correlation between this seminal variability, dormancy, germination and seedling vigor were determined. The seeds were classified in two size categories (morph I  15.0 mm and morph II < 15.0 mm). To each morph morph-nutritional, germinative, and seedling mass variables were determined. All the parameters differ among morphs except for the seed humidity content and root dry mass. A clear relation existed among the differences in size and mass of the seeds, germinative response and seedling vigor. In both seed morphs exist an exogenous mechanic dormancy combined with endogenous dormancy because insufficient embryo morphologic development. The seeds with bigger size and better nutritional state (morph I) germinated quicker and reached the most seedling vigor, reflected the last one in the shoot and leaf dry masses. In the smallest seeds (morph II) the highest values were obtained in the index of cover seminal mass and in the degree of embryonic dormancy. The possible ecological consequences of the seminal polymorphism are discussed.

The phenological phases analysed were: young, mature and old leaves, young and mature flowers, young and mature fruits, and old and dry branches. The observations were done each 15 days, from the second half of May 1999 until the first half of May 2000. The climate is characterized by a very dry winter and a rainy summer. There are four patterns in the species behaviour: 1.- species with production of new leaves in the rainy season in the summer, the leaf fall occurs at the final of the dry winter, without reproductive phases (Copaifera langsdorffii, Qualea grandiflora, Guettarda viburnioide), 2.- species producing the new leaves at the end of the dry winter season, and beginning in the rainy summer; the production of flowers, fruits and leaf fall along the year (Alibertia edulis, Rudgea viburnoides, Luehea divaricata, Nectandra megapotamica), 3.- species producing the new leaves, flowers and fruits in the beginning of the rain in the summer, fall leaf in the dry winter (Rhamnidium elaeocarpum, Erythroxylum pelleterianum) 4.- species with production of new leaves, flowers, fruits and the fall leaves along the year (Siparuna guianensis). The general behaviour of the ensemble of species is characterized by the increase of the production of leaves, flowers, fruits in the rainy summer and decrease in the dry winter. The increase of fall leaf in the dry season contributes to the semideciduous and seasonal appearance of the forest.

Los grupos mejor representados en el listado son los Hongos Mitospricos y las familias Meliolaceae, Coriolaceae, Hymenochaetaceae, Xylariaceae, Glomaceae, Tricholomataceae y Acaulosporaceae. 42597428|El planeamiento ambiental, dentro o fuera de reas protegidas, es una estrategia para lograr el uso racional de los recursos naturales y la conservacin "in situ" de la diversidad biolgica y alcanzar tanto el bienestar de la sociedad como el desarrollo sostenible. Este trabajo presenta el uso de una metodologa propuesta por Cervantes, 1996, para la Zonificacin Ecolgica Econmica (ZEE) con vistas a resolver los conflictos ambientales y econmicos en un rea ubicada fundamentalmente en la Cuenca del Soldado al Noroeste de la Isla de la Juventud, como un primer paso para llegar al ordenamiento ambiental de la regin de estudio. El proceso de zonificacin permiti identificar cuatro zonas en dependencia de sus potencialidades: Zona I de Conservacin, Zona II de Rehabilitacin, Zona III y IIIa de Aprovechamiento (forestal y minero) y Zona IV de Proteccin Ecolgica. The environmental planning, in or outside of protected areas, is an strategy to obtain the rational use of the natural resources and the conservation "in situ" of the biodiversity with the aim to improve the welfare of the society and the sustainable development. This paper presents the way in which the methodology proposed by Cervantes, 1996 for the Ecological-Economical Zoning (ZEE) allows to solve the environmental and economic conflict in a study region located in Cuenca del Soldado at the Northwest part of the Isle of Youth as a first step to reach to the environmental ordering of this zone. The ecological zoning process allow us to identify four zones, taking into account potentialties: Zone I Conservation, Zone II Rehabilitation, Zone III and IIIa forestal and mining use and Zone IV Ecology preservation.

This case study was conducted as an exploratory research in the small town of Santiago de Anaya, Mexico. Selected, was three of the most representative events of the community which centered on gastronomy. A questionnaire was applied with the purpose of finding out the most characteristic daily dishes of the town throughout the last 40-50 years; and to determine if there were any changes in gastronomical intake during this period of time. Therefore, a better recognition/publicity of the gastronomical activities of Santiago de Anaya, could possibly transform these cultural event into a popular tourist attraction.

Por otra parte, el uso de la microscopa electrnica revela marcadas variaciones en la estratificacin de la exina; caracteres tales como: capa basal, estructura del infratecto y presencia de microcanales o microprocesos supratectales, investigados en siete especies de Arecaceae, corroboran que existen suficientes modificaciones del tcto y en la estructura de la exina, para ser evaluadas en la identificacin de material fsil o melisopalinolgico. Trichotomosulcate pollen grains in fourth out of 15 genera of Cuban Arecaceae are reported in addition to a different aperture configuration in Coccothrinax litoralis and Coccothrinax salvatoris pollen grains. Taxa that share monosulcate and trichotomosulcate pollen are Pseudophoenix sargenta, Gastrococos crispa and Bactris cubensis whereas Acrocomia aculeata has only trichotomosulcate pollen grains. The palynological meaning of trichotomosulcate condition is discussed. On the other hand, the electron microscope techniques show outstanding variation in exine stratification, when tested in seven species of Arecaceae. Features such as basal layer, infratectum structure and microchannels or supretectum microprocesses corroborate thattectum modifications and exine structure exist to such extent as to be assessed in the determination of fossil or melissopalynological samples. Structure variations in pollen wall of Coccothrinax crinita and Coccothrinax salvatoris reveal that detailed research in large genera should be continued.

42597211|Se discute el papel de los patrones de nerviacin del pecolo y de la hoja, la evolucin de la apertura del grano de polen y los caracteres de la exina en Buxus en relacin con su disyunta distribucin global y la clasificacin del gnero. La notable evolucin paralela de la apertura del polen y los caracteres de la exina en los diferentes continentes sirve de base a esta agrupacin y se interpreta como expresin de un ancestro bsico comn. Por el contrario, los patrones de nerviacin de la hoja reflejan claramente la diferenciacin evolutiva entre los grupos continentales y dentro de ellos. Patterns of leaf petiole and axis vascularization, of pollen grain aperture evolution and exine characters as well as characters of leaf venation of Buxus are discussed in relation to the disjunct global distribution and classification of the genus. The most original taxa are represented in Eastafrica, while three independent branches with clearly separated phyletic groups occur in America, in East Asia and in South Africa. The remarkable parallel evolution of aperture and exine characters on the different continents support this grouping and is interpreted as expression of a common ancestral genetic basis. In contrast the patterns of leaf venation clearly reflect the evolutionary differentiation between and within the continental groups. Cuba represents the evolutionary centre in the New World with the highest number of species and the greatest morphological and phylogenetical diversity, from where only few phyletic groups seem to have migrated to the other Antilles and Central America.

42597216|El trabajo presenta una serie de mapas paleogeogrficos que ilustran la formacin y evolucin del Caribe desde el Trisico Tardo al presente y se discuten sus implicaciones biogeogrficas. Quizs desde el Bathoniano (=164 Ma), pero ciertamente desde el Oxfordiano (=154 Ma), los datos de la estratigrafa indican que esta conexin era totalmente funcional y la corriente marina Circum-Tropical estaba activa. La dispersin de las biotas terrestres entre Laurasia occidental (Amrica del Norte) y Gondwana occidental (Amrica del Sur) se interrumpi desde el Calloviano, cuando entre esos continentes se form una faja de mar que los separ. Posteriormente hubo intercambios de tetrpodos entre Amrica del Norte y Amrica del Sur, a travs de un puente terrestre que los conect brevemente durante el Campaniano tardo y el Maastrichtiano (=75-65 Ma), y a partir del Plioceno (2.5-2.3 Ma). Las evidencias de que haya existido un puente intracontinental al final del Mioceno Medio aun es ambigua. Desde la formacin del primer archipilago de islas volcnicas en el rea del Caribe, aproximadamente en la transicin jursico-cretcico (=141 Ma), en el escenario paleogeogrfico del Caribe y su entorno han estado presentes islas volcnicas, bajos, y crestas. Pero aquellas tierras emergidas fueron generalmente efmeras, ya que se sumergieron apenas unos pocos millones de aos despus de emergidas; y si soportaron alguna biota, estas desaparecieron junto con las islas. Slo a partir del eoceno medio (=40 Ma) han existido tierras permanentemente emergidas en el marco geogrfico del Caribe, que proveen el substrato necesario para la formacin y desarrollo de las biotas terrestres actuales. De particular importancia biogeogrfica en este periodo de tiempo, fue la formacin de una extensa cresta emergida (Gaarlandia), que hace 35-33 Ma uni brevemente Amrica del Sur con los ncleos de las futuras Antillas Mayores, y el desarrollo de los ncleos terrestres antillanos hasta el presente. Since latest Triassic the Caribbean started to be formed as a system of Jurassic rift valleys within west-central Pangaea, later evolving into a mediterranean sea where distinct volcanic and non volcanic island evolved. Since its very early formation this sea has been playing an important roll controlling the historical patterns of ocean water circulation, moderating the world climate, and determining the possibilities of biotic exchange of the surrounding terrestrial and marine ecosystems. The formation of a Mesozoic marine seaway between the western Tethys and the eastern Pacific, across west-central Pangaea, has been postulated for the Early Jurassic (Hettangian-Pliensbachian) according to biogeographic thesis, but supporting stratigraphie data is lacking. Probably since the Bathonian but certainly since the Oxfordian, the stratigraphie records indicate that this connection was fully functional and the Circum Tropical marine current was active. Overland dispersal between western Laurasia (North America) and western Gondwana (South America) has been interrupted since the Callovian when the continents were separated by a marine gap. Later, a connecting landbridge may have been present during the latest Campanian/Maastrichtian (=75-65 Ma), and since the Plio-Pleistocene (2.5-2.3 Ma). Evidence for a precursor bridge late in the Middle Miocene is ambiguous at this time. Since the formation of the first volcanic archipelago within the Caribbean realm, at about the Jurassic-Cretaceous transition, volcanic islands, shallow banks, and ridges have been present in the paleogeographic scenario of the area. But these lands were generally ephemeral, as they lasted just a few million years. Only after the Middle Eocene (< 40 Ma ago) permanent lands were present within the Caribbean geographic scenario, providing the substrates for the formation and development of the present terrestrial biota.
42597217|El afloramiento de serpentina de "lomas de La Coca" es probablemente una de las localidades serpentincolas ms estudiadas de Cuba. Sin embargo, la complejidad florstica y fisonmica presentes en la misma, ha motivado discrepancias entre los resultados de diferentes autores. En este trabajo, se discuten los criterios seguidos en los estudios anteriores sobre la zona y se describen las formaciones vegetales primarias y secundarias considerando su relacin con factores abiticos como el tipo y la profundidad del suelo y la exposicin. Las formaciones primarias definidas y caracterizadas para esta localidad son el bosque semideciduo microfilo sobre serpentina, el matorral xeromorfo espinoso sobre serpentina y el bosque de galeria. Los tipos de vegetacin secundaria estn representados por el matorral xeromorfo espinoso sobre serpentina degradado, el herbazal secundario con arbustos y palmas, el bosque de galeria sobre serpentina degradado y el herbazal secundario con Cecropia schreberiana. The serpentine outcrop of "lomas de La Coca" is one of the more studied serpentine area in Cuba. However, its complex flora and vegetation have conduced to contradictories results. In this work we discuss previous results and propose vegetation units based on biotic and abiotic factors such as: aspect, soil type and soil deep. The primary defined vegetation types are the microphyllous semideciduos forest on serpentine soil, the thorny xeromorphic shrubwood on serpentine soil and the gallery forest. Secondary vegetation types are represented by disturbed thorny xeromorphic shrubwood on serpentine soil, grassland with shrubs and palms, disturbed gallery forest and grassland with Cecropia schreberiana.

42597219|Se estudia el sinantropismo en la flora de la localidad Tetas de Juana, Alturas de Banao, en el macizo montaoso Guamuhaya de Cuba Central. Se determina el comportamiento de las especies sinantrpicas referidas para esta rea y se aplica la clave para determinar las especies sinantrpicas en Cuba; las especies determinadas bajo esta categora se comparan con la lista de especies sinantrpicas publicada para Cuba. Se reportan un total de 152 especies sinantrpicas de las cuales 138 son espermatfitos, la mayora de estos nativos o endmicos (apfitos), 10 espermatfitos introducidos (antropfitos) y dos de origen desconocido (parapfitos); por su parte los pteridfitos estn representados por 14 especies sinantrpicas, 11 nativas y el resto introducidas. Se reportan 41 especies sinantrpicas nuevas para la flora cubana de ellas el 93% nativas. Se define por primera vez que las especies nativas pueden poseer ms de una categora sinantrpica. Se demuestra que las especies sinantrpicas no se comportan del mismo modo en todos los ecosistemas ni localidades del pas. Se evidencia que el anlisis del fenmeno del sinantropismo debe ser casustico para cada localidad, rea geogrfica o ecosistema. The sinantropism in the flora of Tetas de Juana, located at Alturas de Banao, Guamuhaya massif, is studied. According to the list of the local flora, the behavior of species as sinantropic was determined. In order to determine the sinantropic species, the key of sinantropism was applied to the list. A total of 152 sinantropic species, including spermatophytes and pteridophytes, is reported. The sinantropic spermatophytes are represented by 138 species, most of them native or endemic (apophytes), as well as 11 introduced species (antropophytes) and two unknown species (parapophytes). On the other hand, pteridophytes are represented by 14 sinantropic species, 11 native species and the rest introduced. Forty one new sinantropic species for the flora of Cuba, with 93 % native, is reported. It is defined for the first time that native species can possess more than one synanthropic categories. It is demonstrated that sinantropic species do not behave the same way in each ecosystem or locations throughout the country. Evidences about the casuistic nature of sinantropism in each location, geographic zone or ecosystem, are given.

Se realizaron colectas que se caracterizaron morfolgicamente in situ y en condiciones ex situ durante 2001-2004 teniendo en cuenta los descriptores que recogen la mxima variabilidad presente en el pas. Se describe el lugar de colecta y se reporta la presencia del tipo silvestre estolonfero sobre la superficie de rocas con permanente flujo de agua, y se discuten adems las posibles hiptesis que explican su presencia en Cuba. Las accesiones colectadas poseen ms de 1 m de largo en sus estolones y poseen pecolos y limbos de color verde. Se encontraron algunas diferencias en las coloraciones de races y yema, y se discute sobre la conservacin y uso de estas accesiones por parte de los agricltores. El hallazgo del tipo estolonfero silvestre en la regin oriental de Cuba abre nuevas perspectivas investigativas, ya que contradice la idea de que esta regin del pas es la de menor variabilidad en esta especie. Colocasia esculenta presents the highest variability in central and western Cuba. In 2000 and 2001 we visited non explored zones in eastern Cuba to find evidence of high variability. The samples were morphologically characterized in situ and ex situ in 2001-2004 using descriptors of the highest variability in the country. The locations were described and a stolonipherous wild type growing on rocks with permanent water flow was reported. Several possible hypotheses explaining their presences in Cuba are discussed. The collected accessions have green petioles and leaves and their stolons are more than 1 m long. Some differences in the colour of roots and buds were found. The conservation of the accessions and their use by farmers are discussed. The finding of a stolonipherous wild type in eastern Cuba opens new research perspectives, as it contradicts the belief that this region has the poorest variability in the species.

42597254|Entre las especies de Ficus cultivadas en Cuba y frecuentes en el ambiente urbano, se reconocen como naturalizadas a F. benghalensis, F. microcarpa y F. religiosa las cuales se reproducen por semillas por contar con sus polinizadores especficos, a diferencia de F. auriculata, F. benjamina, F. elastica y F. lyrata solo propagadas vegetativamente. Se identifican como avispas polinizadoras Agaoninae (Hymenoptera, Chalcidoidea, Agaonidae) de F. benghalensis, F. microcarpa y F. religiosa a Eupristina masoni, Eupristina verticillata y Pleistodontes greenwoodi respectivamente, las que adems constituyen nuevos registros (gneros y especies) para Cuba. The main cultivated species of Ficus in Cuba were studied. The presence of pollinating wasps and seed production made possible the recognition of F. benghalensis, F. microcarpa y F. religiosa as naturalized species unlike F. auriculata, F. benjamina, F. elastica and F. lyrata, only reproducible by vegetative multiplication, all of them common in urban environment. The pollinating wasps Agaoninae (Hymenoptera, Chalcidoidea, Agaonidae) Eupristina masoni in F. benghalensis, Eupristina verticillata in F. microcarpa and Pleistodontes greenwoodi in F. religiosa were identify as new reports for Cuba. Except for 2 species, all the endangered ones are endemic. These species grow in 9 plant communities: 6 of them in forests, 2 in thickets and 1 in herbaceous areas. The threat factors for these species are diverse: dominance by the endemics, the insular flora's sensibility, its high aesthetic value, the overexploitation of species of economic value and the reduction of the populations due to environmental modifications, which have lead to the deterioration or destruction of their habitats

42597275|El manejo de semillas a pequea escala es un rea de estudio marginal, sin embargo es una fuente inagotable de variabilidad gentica y conocimientos tradicionales. Por ser Phaseolus lunatus un cultivo subutilizado en Cuba, el objetivo del presente trabajo fue determinar la variabilidad morfo-agronmica de las poblaciones presentes en el pas, y como ella es manejada y conservada in situ por las comunidades rurales. Para ello se caracterizaron 55 accesiones, procedentes de las regiones occidental (10), central (15) y oriental (30), utilizando 30 descriptores morfo-agronmicos. Se utiliz el Anlisis de Conglomerado con el clculo de la distancia euclidiana (D) con el objetivo de observar como se agrupaban por su similitud (S=1-D) las diferentes accesiones evaluadas. De acuerdo a las similitudes encontradas entre las accesiones analizadas se definieron seis grupos morfoagronmicos, con caractersticas distintivas entre ellos. Adems se analiz la informacin sobre el manejo del cultivo, tomada durante las entrevistas realizadas a las familias de las fincas. Se demuestra la existencia de una variabilidad infraespecfica del cultivo de Phaseolus lunatus en Cuba, que los campesinos han mantenido, conservado y manejado hasta nuestros das a travs de su uso, y no ha sido explotada comercialmente hasta el presente, a pesar de poseer buen comportamiento para algunas caractersticas productivas. Because Phaseolus lunatus is a neglectec crop in Cuba, the objective of the present work was determine the morpho-agronomic variability of Cuban populations and how it is in situ managed and conserved for the rural communities in the country. For that 55 accessions from western (10), central (15) and eastern (30) regions were characterized, using 30 morpho-agronomic descriptors. The Cluster Analysis was used and euclidian distance (D) was calculated with the objective to observed how the evaluated accessions were grouped according its similarities (S=1-D), and six groups were defined with distinctive characteristics between them. Also the information extracted from interviews with rural families on crop management was analized, and it was demonstrated the existent of an infraespecific variability for Cuban Phaseolus lunatus crop, that farmers have been maintained conserved and managed through its used until our days, but it has not been commercially exploited in the country at present, even it has good behaviour to productive characteristics.

42597401|Se discute la gnesis de los suelos pardos de Cuba, considerndose como suelos Pardos Mediterrneos decapitados, que en un principio se haban desarrollado en las regiones alomadas de la Isla durante la larga glaciacin wisconsiana en un clima mediterrneo seco y vegetacin arbustiva abierta. La erosin masiva de casi todos los suelos de las zonas alomadas y premontanas de Cuba ocurri durante la transicin del Pleistoceno al Holoceno cuando las lluvias anuales se incrementaron de manera abrupta antes de que la nueva vegetacin forestal climax pudiera cubrir la superficie de la tierra protegiendo al suelo de la erosin. It is exposed the genesis of the brown soils of Cuba: these are considered as truncated Brown Mediterranean soils developed on the hilly lands of the Island during the long Wisconsin glacial period in a dry Mediterranean climate and open shrub vegetation. The massive erosion of almost all hilly and premountain soils in Cuba occurred during the Pleistocene-Holocene transition when the annual rains abruptly increased before the new forest-climax vegetation could cover the land surface protecting the soil from erosion.

42597408|En 1802, arrib a La Habana, procedente de Espaa, Juan Jos Daz de Espada y Fernndez de Landa, que haba sido nombrado Obispo de la Ciudad. Hombre de amplias miras, contribuy al desarrollo de La Habana y a la expansin de la cultura. A l se deben las reparaciones en la catedral habanera, la construccin de El Templete, el apoyo dado a Toms Romay en la expansin de la vacuna contra la viruela, las reformas de la enseanza en el Seminario de San Carlos y San Ambrosio; y la construccin del cementerio que llev su nombre, y que elimin la costumbre de enterrar en las iglesias. La vivienda estaba enclavada entre rboles coposos y rodeada de flores; con predominio del neoclsico de lnea griega y contaba con calles flanqueadas por hileras de mango, que propiciaban el sosiego de la sombra bajo la luz solar; y otras, entre bambes, daban acceso a parques, que por lo amplios, recordaban los predios recoletos de viejos feudos europeos. Estaba abierta al pblico que poda contemplar en ella plantas exticas que el Obispo introdujo, y era punto obligado de visita de los extranjeros que llegaban a Cuba. Sin duda alguna, una de nuestras primeras colecciones de plantas abierta al pblico. In 1802, Juan Jos Daz de Espada y Fernndez de Landa arrived in to Havana from Spain. He had been appointed as Bishop of the City. He was a wide view man. He contributed to the development of Havana City and the cultural expansion in it. He was a man who renovated the Cathedral of Havana and built The Templete. He leaned Toms Romay in the expansion of the vaccine against smallpox. He also organized reforms in San Carlos and San Ambrosio Seminary, built the cemetery that got his name after and he eliminated the custom of burring people on churches. However, nothing of just a little is known about "The Bishop Villa", a country house that Bishop had in Havana's outskirts. The house was built among strong trees and surrounded by flowers, with the predominance of the Greek neoclassical style and it had streets with blossoms and mango that brought about the calm under the shade of the sunlight and others, between bamboo trees with access to wide parks that brought memories about the quiet properties of the old European feuds. It was opened to the public that could looked at different exotic plants introduced by the Bishop in it and it was a forced point of view to the foreign that came to Cuba. Without a doubt, one of our first collections of plants opened to the public.

23725914|Las especies cubanas del gnero Cyrilla se pueden separar en dos grupos segn el reflejo en la haz: cinco especies (C. cubensis, C. macrocarpa, C. megaphylla, C. microareolata, C. nipensis) presentan superficies brillantes, en mayor o menor grado; mientras que las tres especies restantes (C. coriacea, C. lutgardae, C. silvae) presentan superficies opacas; el envs de todas las especies es opaco. Otra caracterstica macroscpica es la presencia de reas pruinosas (blancas) en el pecolo y las lminas foliares (C. megaphylla, C. microareolata, C. silvae). Estas caractersticas foliares fueron examinadas al microscopio estereoscpico y al MEB (Microscopio Electrnico de Barrido). Bajo el microscopio estereoscpico fueron encontradas costras y finas agujas de cera en las reas correspondientes a las reas pruinosas. Al MEB se encuentran en ambas epidermis clulas pentagonales o tetragonales; las superficies con "brillo" en la haz son lisas y las paredes periclinales externas de las clulas epidrmicas son convexas; las superficies sin "brillo" son rugosas o con pliegues y las paredes periclinales externas de las clulas epidrmicas son cncavas. Como estructuras de ceras epicuticulares se observ la presencia en ambas superficies foliares de laminillas enteras o irregulares (laciniadas) y varillas poligonales en las reas pruinosas. Hay sintopismo al encontrarse dos tipos de ceras epicuticulares en la misma superficie. La naturaleza de la superficie epidrmica y la presencia o no de ceras epicuticulares en la misma influyen decisivamente en el "brillo" de la haz. No se encuentra relacin directa entre la presencia o no de "brillo" en la haz y en el tipo de formaciones vegetales en que habitan. Estas estructuras de las superficies epidrmicas foliares se registran por primera vez en el gnero Cyrilla. The Cuban species of Cyrilla can be divided into two groups according the luster of the adaxial leaf surface. Five species (C. cubensis, C. macrocarpa, C. megaphylla, C. microareolata and C. nipensis) exhibit shiny surfaces, while the remaining three (C. coriacea, C. lutgardae, C. silvae) have dull surfaces. The abaxial leaf surface in all species is dull. Another macroscopic foliar feature is the presence of pruinose (white) areas in petioles and blades (C. megaphylla, C. microareolata, C. silvae). These features of the foliar surface were examined under the stereoscopic microscope and scanning electron microscope (SEM). Under the stereoscopic microscope, wax crusts and thin waxy needles were observed in the areas that correspond to pruinose (white) areas. SEM studies revealed in the epidermis of both surfaces pentagonal and hexagonal cells; in shiny adaxial leaf the surface is smooth, the external periclinal epidermical cell walls are convex, while in dull surfaces are rugose or bended, the external periclinal cell walls are concave. Epicuticular wax estructures are: entire and irregular (laciniate) platelets and polygonal rodlets in the pruinose (white) areas in both foliar surfaces. Syntopism was observed since two types of epicuticular waxes were found in the same foliar surface. There are not relationship between the luster in the adaxial surface and the type of vegetation of these plants grow. These structural features of the foliar epidermal surface are reported for the first time in the genus Cyrilla.

23725921|El gnero Leptocereus comprende una docena de especies endmicas del Caribe, la mayora de las cuales son cubanas y todas se encuentran amenazadas de extincin.
